#[CORVETTE] Chemical Thrusters
utility_component_template = {
	key = "SHIP_THRUSTER_1"
	size = small
	icon = "GFX_ship_part_ukn_thruster_1"
	icon_frame = 1
	power = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_power
	
	modifier = {
		ship_base_speed_mult = @ukn_t1_thruster_speed_mult
		ship_evasion_add = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_evasion
	}
	resources = {
		category = ship_components
		cost = {
			minerals = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_cost_minerals
			alloys = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_cost_alloys
#			ukn_meta_materials = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_cost_ukn_meta_materials
#			ukn_femtomatter = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_cost_ukn_femtomatter
#			ukn_condensics = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_cost_ukn_condensics
#			ukn_quasi_matter = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_cost_ukn_quasi_matter
#			ukn_causalitons = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_cost_ukn_causalitons
#			exotic_gases = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_cost_exotic_gases
#			rare_crystals = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_cost_rare_crystals
#			volatile_motes = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_cost_volatile_motes
#			ehof_sr_negative_mass = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_cost_ehof_sr_negative_mass
#---
#			ukn_meta_materials = @ukn_corvette_t1_armor_cost_ukn_meta_materials
#			nanites = @ukn_corvette_t1_armor_cost_nanites
#---
#			ukn_meta_materials = @ukn_corvette_t1_shields_cost_ukn_meta_materials
#			volatile_motes = @ukn_corvette_t1_shields_cost_volatile_motes
		}
		upkeep = {
#			energy = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_upkeep_energy
			minerals = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_upkeep_minerals
			alloys = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_upkeep_alloys
#			ukn_meta_materials = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_upkeep_ukn_meta_materials
#			ukn_femtomatter = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_upkeep_ukn_femtomatter
#			ukn_condensics = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_upkeep_ukn_condensics
#			ukn_quasi_matter = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_upkeep_ukn_quasi_matter
#			ukn_causalitons = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_upkeep_ukn_causalitons
#			exotic_gases = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_upkeep_exotic_gases
#			volatile_motes = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_upkeep_volatile_motes
#			sr_dark_matter = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_upkeep_sr_dark_matter
#			ehof_sr_negative_mass = @ukn_corvette_t1_thruster_upkeep_ehof_sr_negative_mass
		}
	}

	prerequisites = { "tech_thrusters_1" }
	component_set = "thruster_components"
	size_restriction = { corvette colonizer lithoid_colonizer lithoid_colonizer sponsored_colonizer constructor science transport crisis_corvette }
	upgrades_to = "SHIP_THRUSTER_2"

	ai_weight = {
		weight = 1
	}
}
